'''Kokoala''' is a {{Type|Grass}}-type Pokémon.

==Pokédex entry==

{{Dex|type1=Grass
|It's lazy, and spends most of its life clinging to trees. It's very unintelligent and clumsy, so it often ends up falling. Its tough skull is developed to protect itself from these falls. Its nose generates a liquid that allows it to survive weeks without hunting for food.}}

==Pokédex entry==

{{Dex|type1=Grass|type2=Dark
